ESP32-S3 FIRMWARE EXTERNAL CODE COMMENTS

Purpose:
This file stores code comments/docstrings extracted out of the runtime source files so the MicroPython files uploaded to the ESP32-S3 stay smaller.

Runtime build base:
esp32s3_firmware_comment_external_2_0_8.zip

Current synchronized build:
esp32s3_firmware_2_0_9_lite_server.zip

Comment source:
esp32s3_firmware.zip

Extraction summary:
Base externalized comments from 2.0.8 are preserved below.
2.0.9 adds the synchronized change notes in this section and keeps runtime Python comments out of the uploaded code.

Important:
The upload script excludes this .txt file from the ESP32-S3 upload. Keep it on the PC as a reference document.



===== 2.0.9 synchronized external comments / change notes =====
[config.py] VERSION is now 2.0.9-esp32s3-native-370-memfix-lite-server.
[config.py] ENABLE_CAPTIVE_DNS is now False to avoid allocating the extra DNS socket and DNS receive buffers during low-memory startup. Captive-portal HTTP probe paths are still answered by the HTTP server.
[config.py] HTTP_CLIENT_TIMEOUT_MS is reduced from 30000 ms to 3000 ms so a stalled browser connection cannot hold memory for too long.
[main.py] RinaChanApp now uses __slots__ to remove the per-instance attribute dictionary and save heap before protocol_server is imported.
[main.py] initialize() now prints heap free-memory checkpoints before protocol_server import, after import, and after server begin. These numbers are diagnostic only and do not affect protocol behavior.
[protocol_server.py] The server was replaced with a lite implementation. It keeps HTTP, UDP, Web UI file serving, /api/status, /api/state, /api/battery, /api/faces, /api/cmd, /api/send, /api/request, /api/binary, and Wi-Fi status/save/scan endpoints. It removes the in-module DNS responder and reduces large literal strings.
[protocol_server.py] ProtocolServer now uses __slots__ to reduce heap use.
[protocol_server.py] HTTP response files are streamed in small chunks instead of loading the full file into RAM.
[network_manager.py] NetworkManager now uses __slots__ to save heap while keeping the same AP/STA startup behavior.
[upload_and_run_esp32s3.ps1] The uploader now uses a runtime Python allowlist. Helper/source modules remain in the ZIP, but only modules imported by main.py are copied to the ESP32-S3. This removes unused files from the device filesystem after the erase step.
[upload_and_run_esp32s3.ps1] Documentation, external comments, PowerShell files, Markdown files, and CPython cache files are still kept on the PC and excluded from the board upload.
[webui/app.js.gz] JavaScript comments were stripped from the gzipped Web UI bundle and retained externally in this text file, reducing the gzipped asset from about 56.8 KB to about 45.1 KB.

[line 8] [comment] # Pre-activate WiFi interfaces before any other large allocations.
[line 9] [comment] # On ESP32-S3, the WiFi stack needs a contiguous block of internal DRAM.
[line 10] [comment] # If NeoPixel RMT buffers or module bytecode are allocated first the heap
[line 11] [comment] # becomes too fragmented and network.WLAN() raises OSError: WiFi Out of Memory.
[line 12] [comment] # Calling .active(True) here reserves that RAM at the earliest possible moment.
[line 13] [comment] # 逻辑: 下面的操作可能因为硬件、文件、网络或数据格式失败，所以先尝试执行。

[line 18] [comment] # 逻辑: 捕获失败并进行降级/记录，避免单次异常导致固件主流程停止。

[line 5] [comment] # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
[line 6] [comment] # brightness_modes.py
[line 7] [comment] #
[line 8] [comment] # Mode-dependent brightness helpers.
[line 9] [comment] #
[line 10] [comment] # The user-facing brightness value is always stored as a percent in the range
[line 11] [comment] # BRIGHTNESS_MIN..BRIGHTNESS_MAX (5..100) in 5% steps. That percent is mapped
[line 12] [comment] # into a raw per-channel LED cap via BRIGHTNESS_MAX_CHANNEL (170), so at 100%
[line 13] [comment] # the physical output of each channel is capped at 170 and the maximum color
[line 14] [comment] # the board will ever drive is (170, 170, 170).
[line 15] [comment] #
[line 16] [comment] # Face mode uses the full mapped cap.
[line 17] [comment] # Bad Apple is excluded; matrix demo is disabled in the integrated build.
[line 18] [comment] #
[line 19] [comment] # Example (UI 90%):
[line 20] [comment] # - face mode applies    cap = round(90 * 170 / 100) = 153
[line 21] [comment] # - Bad Apple applies    cap = 153 // 3              = 51
[line 22] [comment] # - matrix demo applies  cap = 153 // 3              = 51
[line 23] [comment] # ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
[line 31] [comment] # 依赖说明: brightness_modes.py::clamp_ui_brightness 需要 无直接项目依赖，仅使用内置语法/局部变量。

[line 10] [comment] # Fallback AP. Password must be at least 8 characters for WPA/WPA2.


======================================================================
VERSION 2.0.10 EXTERNAL CHANGE COMMENTS - AP WI-FI STABILITY
======================================================================
- config.py: VERSION updated to 2.0.10-esp32s3-native-370-ap-stable.
- config.py / wifi_config.py: AP SSID changed to RinaChanBoard-S3-AP so clients do not reuse an old saved profile from the previous WPA/WPA2 mixed-mode AP.
- config.py / wifi_config.py: AP_AUTHMODE changed from 4 to 3. This makes the access point WPA2-PSK only instead of WPA/WPA2 mixed mode, which is more compatible with common phones and Windows Wi-Fi clients.
- config.py / wifi_config.py: AP channel changed from 6 to 1. This keeps the AP on a basic 2.4 GHz channel and avoids stale channel cache issues.
- main.py: ProtocolServer is now imported before AP startup while heap is higher. If import or socket allocation still hits MemoryError, the exception is caught so the board does not soft reboot and the AP stays active for debugging.
- main.py: Server startup failures now leave the face display and AP running instead of crashing the whole app.
- network_manager.py: AP startup log now prints a direct connect hint including the AP SSID and URL.
======================================================================

- upload_and_run_esp32s3.ps1: Added optional -OpenAP switch. This edits local wifi_config.py before upload to create an open AP named RinaChanBoard-S3-OPEN for emergency client compatibility testing.
